## AP in contractile cells
contractile cells make up majority of [[Anatomy of heart, great vessels, mediastinum structures#Cardiac muscle + histology|Cardiac muscle]]

| Phases                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |                                             |
| :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------- |
| **Resting (-90mv):** <br>positive ions from ==neighbouring depolarised== cells enter, increasing voltage<br><br>**At threshold Depolarisation (-70mv):**<br>Na+ channels open, ==Na+ fast inflow==, sharp increase in voltage<br><br>Immediately after threshold Early Repolarisation:<br>Na+ channel close,  K+ channel open<br>Small amount K+ ions leak out, cause slight decrease in AP<br><br>Plateau Phase:<br>K+ slow out flow, ==Ca2+ in flow==<br>Keep ==AP constant to allow for cardiac muscle to remain contracted== to expel blood from chambers<br><br>Repolarisation: <br>Ca2+ channel close, K+ channel still open, Na+ channel close<br>==Rapid outflow of K+ ions==, restore initial voltage<br><br>Total time of AP longer to allow cardiac muscle relaxation prevent tetanic contraction, sustained contraction, no time for relaxation  -> causing bad blood pump | ![[Pasted image 20250202125327.png \| 450]] |


mechanism explained in [[04c Generation of Action potential]]
